Communist Infiltration Discovered in Changsha Garrison Troops

Battalion Commander Zhang Jiewu Was Originally a Red Bandit

Soldiers and Officers Newly Establish Joint Guarantee Law

Changsha Correspondence: The 3rd Battalion of the Independent Regiment of the 31st Division was stationed in the provincial office of the division at the Yilao School in Juguan Temple, Changsha. Division Commander Tao Guang had gone to Hengzhou, leaving only Deputy Division Commander Zhou Xiwu in the province to oversee rear affairs. Deputy Division Commander Zhou Xiwu became suspicious of Battalion Commander Zhang Jiewu's unusual behavior and frequent interactions with suspicious individuals. A tip-off revealed that Zhang was an important member of the Red bandits, having served as the secretary of the Shishou County Party Committee of the Red Party. In April of last year, he received 5,000 yuan from the Red bandits to purchase guns and ammunition in Hunan to supply the Red bandits. This was intercepted by the local militia in Jiaoluo, Yuezhou. Now serving as a battalion commander, he is in fact carrying out secret orders from the Red Party to conduct military movement work in the province, hoping to seize the opportunity to launch a riot and attack Changsha. Furthermore, Red bandits Fan Shaoying from Jianli and Yu Yeqin from Shishou have brought funds to Hunan and are hiding in Zhang's home, plotting to collude with the military to cause chaos. After receiving the report, Deputy Division Commander Zhou investigated and found that Zhang lived at No. 19 Xinyun Street. He secretly discussed the matter with Peng Zhuo, the director of the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital, and decided that Peng would dispatch a team to Zhang's home for arrest at 2:00 AM on the 11th. At the same time, Deputy Division Commander Zhou secretly mobilized two battalions of troops to surround Zhang's unit in the middle of the night, hoping to wipe them out in one fell swoop. That night, Peng immediately dispatched a team of security guards to arrest Zhang and seven members of his family and detained them at the Public Security Bureau. Zhang's unit was also suddenly surrounded by Zhou's troops, who offered no resistance and surrendered their weapons. It can be said to be swift and efficient. The next day, all the captured personnel and prisoners were sent to the headquarters for interrogation. After investigation by Zhang Fenggang, the director of the Military Law Office, Zhang Jiewu confessed to being a member of the Red bandits, carrying out military movement work, and plotting to cause chaos in Changsha and assassinate key figures. Fan Shaoying confessed to working secretly in Jianli and Shashi, serving as the vice chairman and secretary general of the Huarong Soviet last year, and now being ordered by He Long and Yun Daiying to bring funds to Hunan, hide in Battalion Commander Zhang's home, and instigate military unrest. Yu Yeqin confessed to being the secretary of the Shishou County Committee, being recruited by Battalion Commander Zhang to bring funds to Hunan, planning to secure a position in the Opium Prohibition Bureau or the Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau, and going directly to Yuanjiang to secretly liaise with the Red bandits in Shishou, Huarong, and Anxiang counties. Director Zhang immediately sentenced Zhang, Fan, and Yu to death, tied them up, and executed them outside Liuyang Gate. The remaining prisoners are awaiting separate interrogation and sentencing. Liu Yinggu, the chief of staff acting as the commander of the Fourth Route Army, believed that it was extremely dangerous for the Red bandits to openly infiltrate the regular army, plot to cause trouble, and attack Changsha. He consulted with the military officers in the province and decided that Hunan soldiers would be organized into groups of five for mutual supervision. If one of the five is a Red bandit, all five would be held equally responsible. In addition, a joint responsibility method was established for officers. If a Red bandit is discovered in a platoon, the platoon leader is jointly responsible. If a Red bandit is discovered in a company, the company commander is jointly responsible. This is to be strictly enforced. (May 15)

Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Pacification Army Besieges the Bandit Den of Jinjiazhai

Ji's Division Arrives in Anhui Province, Ge and Li's Divisions Concentrate in Guangshan

Hankou Correspondence: The remnants of Red bandit Kuang Jisun, along with the bandit forces of the pseudo-First Teaching Division Zhou Weijiong, Second Division Xiao Xie, Third Division Qi Deyi, and Fourth Division Liu Ying, fled from Hubei to southern Henan. After being surrounded and suppressed by various armies, they fled to the border of Anhui and took Jinjiazhai as their stronghold. In order to defend against the pursuit and suppression of the National Army, they stationed the main force of Zhou Weijiong's bandit troops in Banzhuyuan, with a small force stationed in the Shuanghe Tangjiahui Nanxi area. The main force of Xiao Xie's bandit troops was stationed in Yangjiadian, with a small force stationed in Yeji. Qi Deyi's bandit troops were stationed in Suxianshi and Zaohe, and Liu Ying's bandit troops were stationed in Beita Banbalitan to prepare for defense. Kuang Jisun himself was stationed in the old nest of Jinjiazhai. Traces of the bandits were also found in the Guangshan and Huoshan areas. Li Mingzhong, the pacification supervisor of the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei border area, believing that the bandits were entrenched and would inevitably cause great suffering to the people, ordered Ji Hongchang of the 30th Division, Zhang Yinxiang of the 31st Division, Ge Yunlong of the 33rd Division, Zhao Guantao of the 6th Division, Dai Minquan of the 25th Division, and Li Yunheng of the 53rd Division to encircle and suppress the bandits in separate routes. Ji's troops served as the vanguard and had already advanced to the border of Anhui. Zhang Yinxiang's division had also followed. Li Yunheng and Ge Yunlong's divisions were completely concentrated in Guangshan on the 15th and were set to depart soon. Zhao and Dai's divisions remained stationed in the Xinyang to Guangshui area. A total of no less than 50,000 to 60,000 troops were participating in the encirclement, suppression, and garrisoning. They will follow the planned plan and implement the encirclement. As soon as the deployment is complete, a general attack order will be issued. Li Mingzhong is still in the capital attending the National Conference and will return to Huangchuan to supervise the suppression after the conference closes. (May 16)

The Ins and Outs of Kailuan Coal Mine Workers' Go-Slow Strike

Mediation Committee Approves Transfer to Tianjin for Handling

Resolution of the Road-Mine Dispute Is Near

Tianjin Correspondence: A month ago, the workers of the Kailuan Coal Mine, believing that the mine's annual operating surplus was around ten million yuan, while the treatment of workers was very harsh, made a request to the mine management to increase the daily wage by two jiao per person. Unexpectedly, the request for a wage increase was not met, but an order to stop work for two days a week was suddenly announced. The workers were even more dissatisfied, because even if the request for a wage increase was granted, it would only increase by about six yuan per month, but now stopping work for two days a week would result in a loss of about six yuan per month. Therefore, they implemented a go-slow strike on the 11th. The Provincial Department of Industry, fearing that the trend would expand after the workers raised the issue of increasing wages, had already requested the Provincial Government to establish a mediation committee in Tangshan before the go-slow strike to seek a solution. It sent staff member Ding Zhanmei to Tangshan to jointly organize with Ning Wu, the director of the Tangshan Public Security Bureau, Zhao Junda and Bo Lanting, representatives of the capitalists (foreigners), and Ni Changsheng and Zhang Yutang, representatives of the workers. On the day after Ding arrived in Tangshan, seeing that the workers had already implemented a go-slow strike, he immediately telegraphed Tianjin to ask for instructions. Wang Shuchang, the chairman of the Provincial Government, believing that there were more than 40,000 workers in Kailuan and that the situation there was extremely complicated, immediately telegraphed the Tangshan Public Security Bureau to order the workers to resume work immediately and at the same time instructed the Kailuan Mining Bureau to cancel the order to stop work for two days a week, pending a more complete solution. The Tangshan Labor Union, after accepting the authorities' persuasion, ordered the workers to resume work and work as usual on the morning of the 14th. At the same time, the Mediation Committee also announced its establishment and convened representatives from both labor and capital to implement mediation. However, Zhao Junda, the representative of the mine management, did not arrive, and Bo Lanting stated that he was not responsible, so the first round of mediation did not result in the mine management implementing the cancellation of the work stoppage order. Now, the capitalists, because there are many workers there and fearing accidents, requested that the Mediation Committee be transferred to Tianjin for handling. Ding Zhanmei, the representative of the Department of Industry, therefore returned to Tianjin to report to the Provincial Government. It is said that the Provincial Government has approved the transfer of the committee to Tianjin, and the workers' representatives will also come to Tianjin in the next few days. However, now that the workers have resumed work, the future consultations will focus on the two issues of the mine management canceling the work stoppage order and improving treatment. As for the cause of this labor-capital turmoil, it was actually caused by the road-mine dispute. It is said that after Hu Ruoyu, the mayor of Beiping, took office as the Kailuan Superintendent a few days ago, he invited Gao Jiyi and Yang Jiali (managers of the Kailuan Mining Bureau) to return to Tianjin. It is likely that the road-mine dispute will be resolved in the near future. (May 16)

The Result of the Joint Investigation by Hunan and Hubei Provinces of the Case of the Changyue Customs

Hubei Provincial Government Requests the Ministry of Finance to Recover Dike Donations

Hankou Correspondence: Regarding the case of Yang Ren of Changyue Customs embezzling dike funds and offering bribes, the Hubei Provincial Government previously sent inspector Zhang Zexiong to Hunan Province to jointly investigate and report with the Hubei Provincial Committee and the Hubei provincial receiver Liu Dejun. Zhang and Liu have now returned to Hubei and specially submitted the results of the investigation to the provincial government on the 15th. All of Yang Ren's malfeasance and bribery are true. A total of more than 200,000 yuan of Hubei Province's dike donations were embezzled. The provincial government proposed 119 meeting discussions to resolve and request the Ministry of Finance to severely recover the funds. The following is a summary of Zhang and Liu's report: "Previously, we were ordered to jointly investigate the Yang Ren case with the Hunan Provincial Committee. We immediately jointly started an investigation with the members of the Hunan Provincial Government and the members of the Ministry of Finance. No one in charge of the customs station was present, and the criminals fled in droves, making it impossible to retrieve documents. We then decided to investigate the various taxes and Hunan Province pier donations received by the Tax Affairs Department. Because Changsha Customs collected dike donations at seven times the pier donations during Mao's term, we calculated it at ten times the amount. The Yuezhou Customs calculated it as 20% of the additional tax. One tael of silver was converted into silver dollars at a price of 1.55. From April to December of the 18th year, January to May, August to November of the 19th year, and January and February of the 20th year, we found that Changsha Customs should collect 700,000 yuan plus 7,284 yuan, 6 jiao, 5 fen, and 4 li. Even if some goods were exempted from donations, calculating the pier donations at ten times the amount and then reducing it by 30%, it should collect 495,099 yuan, 2 jiao, 6 fen, and 4 li. Yuezhou Customs should collect 114,815 yuan, 5 jiao, and 8 fen, 5 li. The total dike donations to be collected by the two customs stations is 822,100 yuan, 0 jiao, 2 fen, and 9 li. Excluding the 459,313 yuan, 7 jiao, and 1 fen paid by the customs station to the Dike Project Management Committee, there is still a shortfall of 362,786 yuan, 5 jiao, and 2 fen, 9 li. Even if the pier donations of Changsha Customs are calculated at ten times the amount and then reduced by 30%, there is a shortfall of 150,601 yuan, 1 jiao, 3 fen, and 9 li in the dike donations to be paid. As for the fabricated loss case, we feel that the deception of this government is too much. According to conversations with various parties, the customs station did not lose any cash. According to the confession of Wang Jingping, a staff member of the customs station, he received 500 yuan in illegal cash, ten times his salary. From this, we can know that the entire loss was fabricated, calculating the embezzled fabricated loss dike donation at 98,785 yuan, 7 jiao, 1 fen, and 6 li. Even if Changsha Customs is calculated at ten times the amount of pier donations and then reduced by 30%, it also embezzled 73,958 yuan, 2 jiao, and 4 li. Other malpractices such as unauthorized exemption or overcharging and private production of joint tickets are not included. That is, the customs station from April to December of the 18th year, January to May, August to November of the 19th year, and January and February of the 20th year, even calculated at 30%, has a total shortfall of 150,601 yuan, 1 jiao, 3 fen, and 9 li, and fabricated loss, also embezzling 73,958 yuan, 2 jiao, and 4 li in dike donations. The total embezzlement of dike project surcharges from this province is more than 200,000 yuan. It is reasonable to submit the evidence list for review." (May 15)

The East Railway Will Connect with Various Railways in the Northeast

The Communications Committee Dispatches Personnel to Contact the East Railway Bureau

Satisfactory Results Have Been Obtained from Both Sides' Talks

Shenyang Correspondence: Zou Zhiqian, the director of the Road Administration Office of the Northeast Communications Committee, along with Guo Xurun, the director of the Jichang and Jidun Railway Bureau, went to Harbin together. It is said that their mission on the surface is to inspect the railways of the Eastern Provinces, but in fact, they have the important mission of contacting the Eastern Railway and the domestic railways of the Northeast for joint transportation. The Communications Committee received a confidential telegram from Li Shaogeng, the acting director of the Eastern Railway, last month, which stated that the Eastern Railway's transportation has been exhausted in recent years, and its business has been depressed. The board of directors and supervisors proposed that in order to reverse the decline and develop, it is necessary to conduct joint transportation with the Northeast railways. Please telegraph for consultation if you agree. Gao Jiyi, the chairman of the committee, has always had an active development plan for the Northeast railways under his jurisdiction and has long had a major plan to connect with Europe and Asia. He expressed great agreement with Li's telegram and consulted with the directors of the Northeast Railway Bureau and the director of the Road Administration Office of the committee, Zou Zhiqian, and the chief of the Second Section, Zou En-yuan, who all agreed. Zou En-yuan also suggested taking this opportunity to propose superior conditions to the Eastern Railway. Gao agreed and instructed the two Zous to draft their opinions and sent Zou Zhiqian and Guo Xurun to Harbin for the first contact. It was also planned that if they entered into specific consultations, Guo Xurun would take the lead, and other cadres from the committee would be transferred to assist him. After Zou and Guo arrived in Harbin, they had long secret talks at the official residence of the Russian director of the Eastern Railway, Lude Yi. Lude Yi hoped to implement joint transportation with the neighboring Hu-Hai and Qi-Ke railways first, and then with other railways. However, the main point of the Communications Committee was to handle all the railways at the same time and proposed three measures: (1) When joint transportation is implemented, the China Eastern Railway must try its best to reduce transportation prices. The purpose of this joint transportation is not only to seek the development of each other, but also to compete with the South Manchuria Railway. It is necessary to reduce transportation prices to attract more customers. (2) The China Eastern Railway is concerned about the construction of various ports (such as Yingkou Huludao Qinhuangdao) by the Northeast railways and must provide financial or material assistance. Most of the export ports in the Northeast are crude and simple due to economic relations, which cannot compete with Dalian and other places. Since the China Eastern Railway is conducting joint transportation with the Northeast railways, the expansion and construction of various ports is essential. (3) If the Northeast railways feel the lack of locomotives and vehicles when implementing joint transportation with the China Eastern Railway, the China Eastern Railway must use vehicle compression methods to find ways to subsidize the lack of vehicles in the Northeast railways to avoid stagnation. Lude Yi, the Russian director of the East Railway, replied separately to this request, saying that for the first item, as long as it is beneficial to both parties, he will try to reduce it as much as possible within the possible scope. For the second item, the China Eastern Railway is currently financially exhausted and may not be able to meet the hopes of the Communications Committee, but it will also do its best to assist. For the third item, the East Railway uses a wide gauge, which is different from the tracks of the Northeast railways, which is not without difficulty. However, various European countries are now using the quasi-axis adjustment method, which allows the axles to move and can be freely expanded and contracted. Technical personnel should consider the design. Finally, he said that as long as the board of directors agrees to the above three items, he has no objection and finally proposed a specific draft plan for Zou to consider. It is said that both parties were quite sincere in this meeting, so they both considered it satisfactory. Now Zou has submitted the situation to Gao for review. (May 14)

Liaoning Province Assists Various Counties with Spring Plowing

Allocates 1.2 Million Yuan to Various Counties

Shenyang Correspondence: The economy of the Northeast has been bankrupt in recent years, and the people's livelihood has been declining. In addition, the west of Liaoning suffered a flood last autumn, and the local financial situation has become even more urgent. The authorities, considering the hardships of the people, allocated a huge amount of 20 million yuan last winter to lend to farmers and merchants to alleviate their urgent needs. Since the new spring, the grain stored by middle-class farmers has mostly been sold at low prices last winter, leaving little surplus grain, and food is insufficient, making spring plowing difficult. At a time when bandits have not been pacified and the Communist Party is lurking, if the people's hardship is not resolved as soon as possible, it will be difficult to secure local security. The Liaoning and Ning Provincial Governments, aware of the situation, decided to allocate 260,000 yuan of the relief funds raised by the flood relief associations to each county based on the severity of the disaster and lend it to each county for spring plowing. For other counties that are feeling the aftermath of the disaster and are experiencing tight financial conditions and are unable to carry out spring plowing, the Department of Civil Affairs was ordered to make overall plans. It is said that a total of 1.8 million yuan is needed for 23 counties. The first batch decided to withdraw 1.2 million yuan of silver dollars from the official silver house and provide assistance to the most important counties and the disaster-stricken counties that have already received assistance due to the insufficient allocation. Spring loans will be repaid in the autumn with reduced interest. Loan procedures should be as simple as possible to avoid delaying the agricultural season. Regulations were also established for the official silver house to handle the loans directly with the county branches according to the amount of each county's share, and the county finance bureau and agricultural association were to issue the loans in their names, with the county government bearing the responsibility for guaranteeing the loans. On the one hand, the finance bureau and agricultural association organized a spring plowing loan assistance office to investigate the number of mu of land that the people in the territory are unable to cultivate and allocate the funds on a per-mu average to households with guaranteed loans, setting the repayment period for November and December of this year. If there are indeed difficulties, it can be postponed for one year. If any borrower privately lends the funds for profit without engaging in spring plowing, and it is discovered or reported, the loan will be recovered, and the borrower and guarantor will be punished to prevent abuses. As for other counties that are not included in the assistance, because their situation is not urgent, they will be considered later after the situation is reviewed in the future. Currently, the counties that have been designated to receive assistance include Faku, Shuangshan, Liaoyuan, Kangping, Lishu, Huaide, Taonan, Xiuyan, Jinchuan, Huinan, Xinbin, Liuhe, Xinmin, Panshan, Jin County, Tai'an, Suizhong, Zhangwu, Heishan, Liaozhong, Beizhen, Xingcheng, Yixian, Jinxi, Changtu, Kaitong, Andong, Tongliao, Tuquan, Zhanyu, etc. (May 15)

The Rescued Miners of Lieshan Have Been Released

The Mining Area is Protected by the Gong Regiment

A dispatch from Bengbu: At the Lieshan Coal Mine in Suxian, earlier this month, an incident occurred involving the arrest of workers by the Li Battalion of the 39th Regiment of the 7th Division of the Suixi Garrison during an inspection of the mining area. Over a thousand miners went on strike as a result. The general manager of the company, Lu Zidong, went to Xu and negotiated with the authorities of the 7th Division, obtaining a promise from the military leaders to instruct the Li Battalion to release the arrested workers promptly. Lu then traveled from Xu to Su to request Gong Chaomei, the regimental commander of the 39th Regiment of the division, to dispatch a unit to protect the mine. Permission was granted, and Lu returned to Bengbu. According to company personnel, Xu Ziqin, the general manager of the Engineering Department in charge of the miners, and over thirty other workers arrested by the Li Battalion of Suixi, have all been released. It is said that work will resume as soon as the troops dispatched by the Gong Regiment arrive at the mine. From this observation, the Lieshan incident seems to have reached a temporary conclusion. However, various party and government organs, public organizations, and local gentry in Suxian have accused the Lieshan mining area of harboring bandits and harming the local area. Therefore, a meeting was specially convened at the Finance Bureau to discuss several countermeasures (these measures were briefly mentioned in yesterday's newspaper). However, according to a Mr. Fu from the Lieshan Coal Mine Company, the recent arrest of miners by the Suixi garrison was entirely due to a misunderstanding. The area around Lieshan is entirely bandit territory, but he believes that none of the mine's personnel are colluding with bandits. The workers who come to the mine all have a chain of guarantors, and he cannot be sure if there are any undesirable elements among them. As for the bandits captured by the garrison with coal dust on their clothes, it is possible that they infiltrated abandoned mine shafts to hide when being pursued by the troops. Furthermore, the mine's police have captured bandits and recovered hostages near the mining area, which shows that they are definitely not harboring bandits. He believes that the local people in Suxian are using this as an opportunity to attack them, and they are not being understanding of the mine. (May 16)

Another letter from the Lieshan Coal Mine Company stated: The reports in the newspapers about the strike at their mine have been vague and may cause misunderstandings. They are providing the following account of the facts to clarify the truth. The area around the mine is inherently bandit territory. Last year, the Second Brigade of the Anhui Provincial Garrison was stationed in the mountains to protect the mine. Later, due to orders to redeploy, they requested the Seventh Division of the Jinpu Railway Garrison Command to dispatch a team for protection. Commander Wang agreed to dispatch them after concentrated training and review. For several months, incidents of kidnapping and robbery have been heard daily near the mining area. Due to the mine's weak police force, they were unable to suppress them. The local gentry, concerned about the increasing harm to the area, pleaded with the Gong Regiment of the Seventh Division to dispatch a team to suppress the bandits. The Li Battalion of that regiment was incredibly brave and captured and killed the bandits in the Caili area, who had been a scourge to the area for a long time. The local people and the mine's employees were deeply grateful. However, when Battalion Commander Li was returning to Suixikou from Caili, his horse was wounded by bandits as he passed through the North Street of the Kunlian mining area. Suspecting that the workers were colluding with the bandits, he arrested over twenty of them. Fortunately, Regimental Commander Gong Liangqing considered both bandit suppression and mine protection, and his officers and soldiers were fair and impartial. After interrogation, they realized that the workers were innocent and released them all. Because the mine has no garrison, they feared that bandits might infiltrate the mine, so they took the opportunity to suspend work to help the local area eliminate banditry. Now the Garrison Command and the Gong Regiment have ordered teams to be stationed at the mine for protection, and banditry can be eliminated from now on. Fearing that rumors may be inaccurate, they are providing this account of the events. May 17.

Totaling Over 8,000 Mu

Jiangsu Provincial Higher Certification Examination

152 Candidates on the First Day

The Jiangsu Provincial Higher Certification Examination began yesterday (the 17th) in the auditorium of the Education Department. There were over 190 seats, with two candidates sharing one seat. The west end of the examination hall was the entrance for distributing papers, and the east end was the exit for collecting papers. Outside was the roll call area. Each area was staffed by dedicated office personnel. Yesterday, 152 candidates arrived, with 24 absent. The first session at 8:00 AM was for Chinese Language, Botany, and Biology. Chairman Ye and Director Hu were both chief examiners. However, Chairman Ye was unable to attend in person due to the National Assembly in Beijing and entrusted Director Hu with full authority. He also appointed Hu Huisheng and Yao Yuanchu as assistant examiners to grade the exam papers. The invigilator was Prosecutor Yan from the court, and there were also eight proctors who patrolled the hall. The security was very strict, and the order was well maintained throughout the hall. The second session at 10:30 AM was for Chinese and Foreign Geography, Zoology, and Physiology and Hygiene, with Examiners Hu Huanyong and Yan Fuqing presiding. The papers were collected and the session ended at approximately 12:20 PM. In the afternoon at 2:00 PM, the subjects were Political Science, Principles of Education, Higher Chemistry, and Chemistry. At 4:30 PM, the subjects were Civil Law, History of Education, and Higher Mathematics. Each session was presided over by the respective examiner. (May 18)

Local Correspondence

Qingpu

The Patrol Team Captures Bandits and Transfers Them to the County: Two net boats were previously docked near Doufubang outside the south gate of our county. The local villagers, finding the boats suspicious, reported it to the Patrol Team. The police were dispatched and captured three bandits on the spot, finding a considerable amount of clothing and items. After a preliminary interrogation at the department, they were transferred to the county government for legal action. A Gale Capsizes a Joss Boat, Killing Over Twenty People: On the 28th day of the third month of the lunar calendar, traditionally the birthday of the Eastern Peak Great Emperor, the pilgrimage to Jinze Town in the Fifth District of the western part of our county is very grand. On this day, pious men and women from all over formed teams to go to the temple to offer incense. Three joss boats came from Xitang. About three li from the town, they were suddenly hit by a gale. All three boats capsized at the same time, and the pilgrims fell into the water. The sounds of people shouting and crying were deafening. Fortunately, people nearby tried their best to rescue them. In the end, over twenty people drowned because they could not be rescued in time.

An Uncle and Nephew from Wangtian Village Were Kidnapped: Dong Yinhang and Dong Yunfei, an uncle and nephew who were residents of Wangtian Village in the Fourth District, were farmers. In recent years, they had accumulated some savings, which attracted the attention of bandits. On the 16th of this month, at midnight, a dozen bandits suddenly came and kidnapped the Dong uncle and nephew, demanding a huge ransom. Their family members are currently trying to rescue them.

Songjiang

The Establishment of the County Prison Advancement Association: The County Government previously received an instruction from the Higher Court, which in turn received an instruction from the Judicial Administration Department, stating that in order to improve the treatment of inmates and to reorganize prison affairs, a County Prison Advancement Association should be established and attached to the County Government. The association would have both ex officio and appointed members. The ex officio members would be the County Magistrate or the Court President and Prosecutor, if there is no court, the trial judge, the presidents of the agricultural, industrial, and commercial associations, the directors of the education and public security bureaus, the district chiefs of this area, and the prison warden. The appointed members would be nominated by three or more of the ex officio members and would be elders, scholars, and party rectification committee members residing in the prison's location. The number of appointed members should not exceed half of the ex officio members. Temporary regulations were also attached to the instruction. County Magistrate Jin convened a meeting on the afternoon of the 18th. The attendees included Court President Huang Liang, Prosecutor Zhu Xiyu, Public Security Bureau Director Shen Jing, First District Chief Zhong Taishi, and Prison Warden Zheng Ligeng. County Magistrate Jin presided over the meeting and decided to organize the association in accordance with the regulations. In addition to designating the above-mentioned officials as ex officio members, local figures Lu Longxiang, Zhang Xiaomei, Cai Zhongyu, and the standing committee members of the County Party Department were nominated as appointed members. The County Government will send letters of appointment immediately and will hold the inaugural meeting on June 1st. It is reported that the association's tasks include raising funds for prison repairs and improving the lives of prisoners. The members will inspect the prison once every two weeks.

This matter was learned by Qin Jieren, the director of the Public Security Bureau, who ordered the chief police officer to strictly arrest Wang Er and bring him to justice.

Transfer of District Chiefs: Pang Shusen, the county magistrate of Kunshan, yesterday ordered Zhang Yi, an autonomous investigation officer, to be transferred to the post of the tenth district chief. Wang Guanchu, the tenth district chief, was transferred to the post of the second district chief. Zhang Yilun, the second district chief, was transferred to the post of autonomous investigation officer. Dai Junong, the third district chief, and Zhu Wenyuan, the fourth district chief, were exchanged. After receiving the orders, the district chiefs were already preparing for the handover.

Suzhou

District Chief Shen Leads a Team to Suppress Lake Bandits: Recently, lake bandits have been appearing in the villages of Wuxian County. Although the water and land police teams have tried their best to pursue and suppress them, they have been running from east to west, causing local worries. On the morning of the 18th, District Chief Shen of the Third Water Public Security District received a report stating that many bandit ships and over a hundred lake bandits had been discovered on the east and west sides of Dongting. District Chief Shen immediately boarded the Zhenwei patrol ship and led a team to suppress them.

Examination of the Tragedy at the Competition: A farmers' competition was held in Xiangcheng Township, and a melee occurred. The township's merchant corps and security corps went to the scene to suppress the violence and fired warning shots. Stray bullets killed a villager named Xi Ashou and drowned a Mr. Lü, and injured over twenty people. It is now learned that the local court sent Prosecutor Lai to the township on the 18th to inspect the scene. It was confirmed that Xi Ashou died from a box gun bullet, and the family was ordered to prepare a coffin for burial. However, it has not been determined whether the merchant corps or the security corps fired the shot, as both had box guns. Two injured people, Li Shoutang and Hou Renchu, came to the city on the 18th and petitioned the local court for an inspection. They also accused Hou Liancheng, an officer of the security corps, of instigating the shooting. It is heard that before the competition, various slogans threatening the government were discovered in the township, such as, "If the county government prohibits the competition, we will all refuse to pay taxes." and "If the Public Security Bureau prohibits the competition, if there is a plague or disease in the township, we will negotiate with the Public Security Bureau." It is said that the person nicknamed "the local emperor" in the township was the initiator of the competition. The court plans to summon the people involved for questioning tomorrow.

Various Industries Acknowledge and Undertake Business Tax Collection: The Wuxian County Trade Associations are taking on the responsibility for Wuxian County's Business Tax collection in its entirety. They are currently investigating the business volume of various industries to facilitate the selection of representatives to negotiate with the Finance Department. As of the 18th, only over thirty industries had been investigated, with an estimated taxable amount of over 22,000 yuan. Over forty industries have not yet reported. The Business Tax Research Committee held a meeting on the 18th and decided to set a deadline of the 25th for reporting. Zhang Shoupeng, Lu Jicao, and Wu Xianglin were selected to contact and urge the industries to report. Wang Shutang, the director of the Wuxian County Business Tax Collection Bureau, went to the County Chamber of Commerce on the 18th to discuss this matter. Cheng Ganqing received him and discussed everything. It has been ordered to collect 2/1000 for silkworm cocoon businesses which will be collected directly by the Collection Bureau.

The Fourth Executive Committee Meeting of the Poor Children's Home: The Suzhou Poor Children's Home is a private charitable organization that has been established for nearly twenty years. Over the years, hundreds of graduates have served in various fields and have been able to support themselves. Yesterday morning, the fourth executive committee meeting of the home was held. Over twenty committee members signed in. Zhang Yunbo presided over the meeting, and after discussing everything, the second standing committee was elected. As a result, Cao Songqiao, Zhang Yunbo, Yang Qianli, Liu Zhengkang, Cheng Ganqing, Pang Futing, and Peng Qianbo were elected. In view of the increasing number of poor children and the increasing financial difficulties, the committee unanimously decided to appoint Li Yinquan, Zhang Zhongren, Shi Shengzhi, Wu Guanghan, Lu Yanting, and Xu Boming as executive committee members to assist.

Wuxi

Stealing Bamboo Shoots Turns into a Tragedy: Wu Rongquan, a villager from the Ditianxia area of the Tenth District, was passing by the Dongqiaotou area in the eastern suburbs yesterday morning when he saw the thriving bamboo shoots in Cao A'gen's bamboo forest. He was tempted by the small profit and entered the forest to dig up the bamboo shoots with a knife, tied them into a bundle, and carried them out of the forest. Suddenly, he was spotted by a villager, someone A, who shouted "Thief!" The villagers in the area heard the sound and rushed to grab Rongquan. Without asking for an explanation, they punched and kicked him. Then they used an iron hairpin to stab Rongquan hard in the left leg. Blood immediately flowed like a fountain, and Rongquan was seriously injured, lying in a pool of blood, gasping for breath, and on the verge of death. The villagers knew they had caused trouble and carried Rongquan to the wheat field in front of Cao Xiang and fled separately. After a while, he was spotted by a passerby, who reported it to the First Sub-District of the direct jurisdiction. Inspector Yu, upon receiving the report, immediately sent a chief police officer to investigate and arrest Cao A'gen, the perpetrator, and then transferred him to the head office for review.

It is Difficult to Expect the Package System to Be Cancelled for Electricity: Tao Nianzu, Yan Juezhi, and 800 households, including the Jingyi Tang and Zhang Yimao stores, in the urban area of our county, requested Director Wu of the Qishuyan Power Plant to respect public opinion, cancel the package system, and restore the original price, as the Wuxi City electricity bill has effectively been 18 cents since May 1st. It is now learned that Director Wu, after receiving the letter, sent Yang Huaigu, the resident commissioner in Wuxi, to visit Yan Juezhi and inquire about everything. After two conversations, the two sides reached an agreement. The power plant believes that at a time when gold is expensive and silver is cheap, the raw materials for electricity are soaring, and coal prices are rising, even canceling the 10% discount would not compensate for the reality. Therefore, there is no room for maneuver regarding the actual receipt of 18 cents. However, they promised that once the price of gold decreases, they will first restore the price to the previous level and then charge a 10% discount as before. If the price of gold rises again in the future and the electricity price increases, they will first seek the consent of the citizens before making an announcement. Mr. Yan believes that although the power plant has adopted public opinion to show goodwill, there is no real guarantee for canceling the package system and abolishing unequal treaties. It is difficult to hope that the electricity price will be cancelled before the price of gold returns. Based on these three points, he still plans to continue to demand to avoid chaos.

A Large Gang of Lake Bandits Looted Fenshuidun: It has been reported in this newspaper that over twenty bandit ships were discovered in the Fenshuidun area at the intersection of Xiwuyi. Mao Mujun, the district chief of the Second District of the Xiwu Water Police, sent the Hongping and Baosu warships to mashan on Taihu Lake to suppress them. It is now learned that there were over thirty lake bandits on the bandit ships, all armed with guns. After arriving in the town, they searched every household. After about two hours, they left with their loot. It is estimated that seven or eight stores, including Sun Shunxing Nanhua store and Qu Shuntai Nanhua store, were looted, with a total loss of approximately one thousand yuan. When the lake bandits left, they kidnapped a certain Ms. Liu, the eldest daughter-in-law of Liu Qinsheng, a resident of the town, and a granddaughter. Wang Wenlin, the owner of the Tongtai Nanhua store, and the young clerk of the Gongshun Hotel, Zhang Jinhai, were also kidnapped to the bandit ship. They immediately set sail, drumming and paddling towards Taihu Lake. Afterwards, the families of those kidnapped were very anxious and hoped that the authorities would find a way to rescue them so that they could reunite with their loved ones.

An Elderly Man in His Sixties Rapes a Young Girl: Ye Ziping, also known as Ye Mazi, a resident of the Kutang Bridge area outside the south gate of our county, is 61 years old and fond of beauty. He currently runs a Kefu lead shop in the area and is financially well-off. The other day, Ye saw Xie Axi, a seventeen-year-old female worker in workshop number 63 of the Taifu Silk Factory under the Taa Bridge. Struck by her beauty, he immediately broke into Axi's room and committed rape. Axi refused and shouted for help. Seeing the situation was bad, Ye immediately fled. At that time, neighbors heard the sound and came to ask what was happening. Axi considered the matter a matter of honor and committed suicide by grabbing a kitchen knife in the kitchen. She was rescued by people and nothing happened. Afterwards, the neighbors reported the information to the third police station of the third branch of the Public Security Bureau. The police took Ye Ziping and Xie Axi to the police station and transferred them to the second branch. After a preliminary trial by Director Wang, Ye Ziping was sentenced for improper conduct and fined seven yuan, and Xie Axi was fined five yuan as a warning. Before both parties left the bureau, the woman Xie Axi, because the suicide attempt was unsuccessful, jumped into the river and tried to drown. She was rescued by people and was not submerged. It is heard that the people of Nanli believe that Ye Ziping dared to rape a woman and actually obstructs local customs. It is planned to file a complaint within the day to serve as a warning.

Danyang

Gangsters Provoke Trouble and Act Violently: Shao Ruiyi, a resident of Beiluo Village in the west of the township, has long had a feud with Zhang Maosong, a gangster from Quanzhou. Zhang has repeatedly thought of retaliating, but has not been able to do so. Yesterday, Shao came to the city to buy cattle. When he went to Situ Temple to take a rest in the tea shop, Zhang learned of it and led many of his gangsters to seize Shao and break his head with an iron weapon. Zhang and the others saw their goal had been achieved and scattered. However, Shao was seriously injured and has been taken to the city for examination. The police team captures a suspect: According to a tip-off, the third squad of the Jiashan police team stationed in the north of the township arrested Zhang Changgeng and Zhang Changyou from Yangzhou County in the area of Longwang Temple on suspicion of robbing Dacheng Bridge. They have been sent to the county government for interrogation.

Nantong

Pursuing and Suppressing Northern-Fleeing Sea Bandits: The sea bandits who caused trouble in the Lvsi, Juegang, and Pengjiatao areas have been suppressed by the anti-bandit military police, and over one hundred bandits have been eliminated. The bandit leader Yan Zhenling and over one hundred remaining bandits fled north in seven ships. On the 17th, the Jiangsu Maritime Guerrilla Force, the Huaihai Maritime Public Security Team, and the Qihai Chongnan Road Water Patrol Team joined forces to pursue and suppress them in the Pincha area. The southern sea is peaceful. The 282nd Regiment in the Lü Jue area returned to Tongcheng on the 17th.

Rickshaw Pullers Have Resumed Work: The rickshaw pullers of Tongcheng opposed the additional donations by the Construction Bureau and went on strike on the 15th. Request for Instructions on Handling the Case of the Body Abandoned by the Daiwa Ship: The Procuratorate of the County Court has interrogated relevant witnesses several times in the case of the body abandoned by the Daiwa ship at Tianshenggang. However, Li Yifu, the person claiming the body, has not yet been summoned, and there is no progress. Gaoyou

A Bandit Attempts Rape and Is Captured: At around 3:00 PM the other day, six bandits suddenly came to the home of Pan Yuchun, a farmer in Panyangzhuang, the seventh district of the county. Each of them was holding a wooden stick and they swarmed in. They overturned boxes and cabinets, stealing clothing, silver, and other items worth over a hundred yuan. One of the bandits, named Zhu Zhengkui, noticed that Pan's daughter-in-law (nicknamed Dalianzi) was beautiful and became lustful. He grabbed Dalianzi and intended to rape her. Pan's wife, Yu, saw this and went outside to beat the gong and shout, "Catch the thieves!" The other bandits also chased after her and grabbed Yu, hitting her hard with a stick, causing her serious injuries. This alarmed the people of the whole village who came to rescue them. They captured Zhu Zhengkui and Chen Jiaming on the spot and reported to the Second Squad of the First Company of the police stationed in Sanzhaozhen. Captain Han sent the two bandits to the police brigade headquarters, which transferred them to the county government for interrogation.

Pinghu

The Tragedy of a Sister-in-Law Gouging Out Her Brother-in-Law's Eyes: Shao Basangguan of Zhujingfang is addicted to opium. As a result, his family property has been exhausted. There is still a house, which he owns jointly with his widowed sister-in-law Shao Tao. Recently, Basangguan secretly dismantled and sold the doors and windows of the house. Tao learned of this and at midnight last night (the 15th), colluded with the local thug Xiao Arong and her brothers to seize Basangguan, beat him severely, gouged out both of Basangguan's eyes with nails, mixed them with lime, and left in a hurry. When neighbors heard the sound and rushed to the rescue, Shao Basangguan's head was swollen like a gourd, a terrible sight.

Detention of Editor of the Republican Daily - The Hefei Republican Daily and Jue Bao newspapers published an article titled "Letter from a Soldier Named Qiu Ba to County Court Clerk Pan and Yuan Regarding Smuggling Opium." The County Court, in addition to sending letters to the two newspapers demanding corrections, dispatched bailiff Sheng Wanzhou and others on the morning of the 12th to summon Liu Yuanchi, the editor-in-chief of the Republican Daily, and Li Yunfei, the editor-in-chief of the Republican Daily. Li Shi was out of the office, but Liu responded to the summons and went. After being interrogated by prosecutor Xie Gongcheng, he was detained. The Journalists Association is currently negotiating for his release.

Discussion on Trade News

Reading Mr. Shang Zhongyi's "Further Discussion on Children's Reading Materials" Made Me Realize That "Talking Birds and Animals" Really Doesn't Need to Be Abolished - Wu Yan Yin

Mr. Shang's "Further Discussion on Children's Reading Materials" seems to be directed at those who "support fantastical fairy tales." However, his answer to my question was not entirely satisfactory. Although not entirely satisfactory, I still find it quite acceptable.

After hastily reading Mr. Shang's work, the atmosphere felt very tense. It seemed as if Chinese elementary school textbooks were full of the "fantastical fairy tales" Mr. Shang mentioned, and many followers of "fantastical fairy tales" were loudly advocating for them. The one raising the question, myself, was portrayed as the chief culprit "supporting fantastical fairy tales." In reality, I can reassure Mr. Shang with a joke: our country's elementary school textbooks have never been like American textbooks. There isn't much material related to "fantastical fairy tales" at all. Textbooks on so-called nature, society, or general knowledge certainly have none, and even in language textbooks, there are very few. As for people who support "fantastical fairy tales," Mr. Shang's essay seems to be targeting me specifically. But Mr. Shang has misunderstood. Although I am unenlightened, I would never become a loyal servant of "fantastical fairy tales." My attitude is the same as Mr. Shang's, believing that we should "carefully select and retain first-rate fairy tales with artistic value and entertainment interest." If Mr. Shang were to look at the various restrictions on selecting materials for language education in the Ministry of Education's Provisional Curriculum Standards for Elementary School Language, he wouldn't have this misunderstanding. It's not that I believe Mr. Shang's remarks are "shooting without a target." In the future, Chinese elementary school textbooks might mistakenly become like American textbooks, filled with "fantastical fairy tales," and I would need Mr. Shang's guidance. Mr. Shang's words make us "choose even more carefully" in the future, which is indeed very good.

The above is a response to misunderstandings in Mr. Shang's "Further Discussion on Children's Reading Materials."

As for what Mr. Shang should have answered me, it is the most crucial question: "Are talking birds and animals the same as supernatural stories?" Mr. Shang did not explicitly answer this question, which I consider not entirely satisfactory.

I believe that some talking bird and animal stories use "personification," while others are natural stories explaining life. They are fundamentally different from the records in "Investiture of the Gods" or "Strange Tales from a Chinese Studio." They cannot be confused with supernatural stories, nor can they be confused with "fantastical fairy tales." Of course, many supernatural stories and "fantastical fairy tales" do involve talking birds and animals, but there are also many talking bird and animal stories with no supernatural elements and not necessarily containing fantasy. For example, the "Hurry, Cuckoo" in bird language poetry encourages farmers, and the questions and answers in "The Cat and the Snail" (see the New Language Textbook, Book 5) explain the snail's life. Where is there any strange or fantastical element in these? Mr. Shang previously confused talking birds and animals with supernatural stories and had an absolute claim that "lower grades… should not use talking bird and animal stories." This time, he again confuses talking birds and animals with "fantastical fairy tales," truly making one mistake after another. However, in this essay, Mr. Shang revealed his agreement with my saying of "no need to abolish" talking bird and animal stories. He said, "Greatly reduce the number of fairy tales, choose even more carefully… stories like 'Elephant Boy' from Jilin might as well be retained." If we examine "Elephant Boy," the elephant talks to ostriches, giraffes, pythons, and crocodiles. It not only has talking birds and animals but also talking snakes and crocodiles. The story that the elephant's trunk was originally short but was pulled long by a crocodile contains supernatural and fantastical elements (see the translation in the book "So It Is" published by Kaiming Bookstore). Someone in China's elementary school education system still dares to use this kind of teaching material, yet Mr. Shang advocates for retaining it, meaning Mr. Shang's approval of talking bird and animal stories is even more advanced than ours. This is powerful proof that Mr. Shang acknowledges the need not to abolish talking bird and animal stories.

Although Mr. Shang did not explicitly answer my question "Are talking birds and animals the same as supernatural stories?", he has indeed approved of talking bird and animal stories. That is why I say that although Mr. Shang's answer is not entirely satisfactory, I still find it acceptable.

Since Mr. Shang approves of talking bird and animal stories, why do I need to say more? I am only afraid that the elementary school education community in our country and the general public concerned about elementary school education have not understood Mr. Shang's intentions and have become confused by our discussions, instead sympathizing with the provincial government chairman's so-called "abolish talking bird and animal stories" rhetoric.

Tragically, just when our country's elementary school textbooks were beginning to "childify," the old society immediately condemned them as "cat and dog textbooks." If we do not recognize Mr. Shang's profound arguments and mistakenly believe that Mr. Shang also opposes "cat and dog textbooks," then textbooks filled with "heaven, earth, sun, moon," "human hands, feet, knife" might be resurrected. If they really are resurrected, the loss to children will be immeasurable.

Finally, I must also ask everyone to pay attention: fairy tales certainly include some myths and animal stories (not all, because many myths and animal stories cannot be considered fairy tales), but there are also two types of animal stories: one containing fantastical elements and the other being natural stories. Although Mr. Shang's remarks are not very supportive of animal stories, he has not opposed "natural stories." If we are to edit elementary school textbooks in the future, don't misunderstand Mr. Shang's meaning and become afraid to use "natural stories." I also hope that Mr. Shang will lead by example and create one or two model Chinese children's reading materials from scratch, so that I can truly understand the "New Garden" in my mind. If he could create one or two textbooks for children across the country to read, I would offer fervent prayers and be delighted for the children of the nation.

As an aside, I am currently rushing to complete a language textbook for lower grades full of natural stories (not avoiding talking bird and animal stories). I have no time to discuss this further. I hope Mr. Shang will, in addition to the question of "Are talking birds and animals the same as supernatural stories and should be abolished?", refrain from making remarks that are not very relevant to this topic. Otherwise, not only will we stray too far from the topic, but I will also not dare to discuss with Mr. Shang again.

Important News

A Record of the Third Day of the Jiangsu Scouting Camp

丨Results of Course Competitions

The First Place in Both Group and Individual Events: Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou High School

The 18th was the third day of the Jiangsu Province Scouting Camp in Zhenjiang. The results of the course competitions are as follows:

The course competitions were held in the rain, divided into group competitions and individual competitions. Each group could participate in up to three items, and each individual could participate in up to two items. The group leader registered the participants in advance with the office. For each competition, there were three announcements before it began. At the start, the referee took attendance three times. Those who were not present after the final roll call were disqualified. All competitions were held in order. The announced results are recorded below:

A. Group

(1) Building a Watchtower: A total of 161 groups and ten other groups participated. They were divided into two groups, with nine people in each group. After the roll call, lots were drawn to determine the order. At the sound of the silver horn, they began construction. Each group had a referee observing their movements. The maximum time limit was 25 minutes to complete the construction. The scoring method was divided into four categories: time, action, stability, and appearance. Time, action, and stability each accounted for 30%, and appearance accounted for 10%. The chief referee was Xue Yuanlong, and the referees were Luo Qiu, Zeng Gansheng, Yang Pinji, Leng Xueqiao, Ma Shaoji, Yuan Zongze, and Lu Zuan. The 60th group (Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou High School) had the best performance. The comparison table is as follows:

(2) Semaphore: A total of 127 groups and fifteen other groups participated, with four people in each group. Divided into senders and receivers. The receivers stood in front of Baota Mountain, and the senders were on a small mound facing Xie. The semaphore consisted of ten characters, with the chief referee determining fifteen different sequences, sealed in envelopes and distributed to each group. After the silver horn sounded, they used two flags to send the message simultaneously. The two receivers wrote the message one after the other. The time limit was no more than 25 minutes after the first group submitted their paper. Scoring was based on time and accuracy, each accounting for 50%. A perfect score was 100. A Record of the Eastern Expedition of the Liangjiang Girls' School Basketball Team (5)

(Sent by Huang Jiping on May 13)

Forfeited in Kyoto First High School Girls丨13 to 6 victory over Nara

Crushing defeat in Kobe First Women's丨Difference of 15 to 16 is One Point

The Eastern Expedition competition comes to an end丨A total of ten matches, six wins and four losses

(Kobe Correspondence) The Liangjiang Girls' School Basketball Team left Osaka for Kyoto at 9:00 a.m. on the 9th to compete with the Kyoto Prefectural First High School Girls' School. Liangjiang forfeited midway because the players were tired from touring the mountains and rivers and could not finish the game. Also, due to being unaccustomed to outdoor competitions, the school warmly entertained them for coming from afar. At 2:00 p.m. on the 10th, they went to Nara at the invitation of the Nara Women's High Normal School and competed. The Nara team was physically strong but had mediocre basketball skills. Liangjiang won 13 to 6. Nara's scenery is beautiful, with three-quarters of the city being parks. They enjoyed their游甚快 very much. That evening, international students Li Li, Yi Xizhen, Gong Junzhu, and Ma Shuqin hosted a banquet to welcome them. On the 11th, they left Osaka and arrived in Kobe at noon. The overseas Chinese provided thoughtful hospitality, and the food and lodging were quite comfortable. At 4:00 p.m. on the 12th, they had a farewell competition with the Kobe First Higher Girls' School for the Eastern Expedition. Each player was nervous, preparing to decide the winner. At that time, the YMCA gymnasium was packed with people, and many overseas Chinese came from afar to cheer them on. At 4:15, the parade began, and then the game started. The first quarter was 4 to 4, with no winner. The second quarter remained the same, with little progress. By chance, the Kobe team took the lead with 11 to 8. In the third quarter, it was 14 to 11. Liangjiang's Shao Jingying suddenly scored four consecutive points, unexpectedly catching up to 15 to 14. However, Kobe then scored another point, and the game was declared over. Liangjiang suffered a crushing defeat of 15 to 16. The referees, Ma Chang and Sawada, were invited to a joint banquet at 6:00 p.m. that evening by the Chinese Consulate General, the Fujian Guild, the Sanjiang Guild, the Guangye Guild, and the Tongwen School. Consul General Zhou gave a sincere speech. At 10:00 a.m. on the 13th, they departed from Kobe for a competition in Seoul, Korea. Mr. Yokoyama, a representative of the Korean News Agency, came to invite them, and the travel expenses were subsidized by the agency. They arrived in Shimonoseki at 9:00 p.m., transferred to a ship to Korea, and arrived in Busan at 10:00 a.m. on the 14th, taking a train directly to Seoul. Three matches were scheduled, and one match was scheduled in Pyongyang. On the 21st, they will go to Shenyang. Liangjiang has a total of ten matches in Japan, with six wins and four losses. Yesterday, Various Circles Commemorated the Martyr Bu Chen Yingshi

Yesterday was the 15th anniversary of the martyrdom of Mr. Chen Yingshi. The Municipal Executive Committee specially convened various circles in the city at 9:00 a.m. in the Municipal Party Headquarters on the third floor to hold a memorial meeting. More than 700 representatives from all walks of life attended. The meeting was presided over by Yang Qingyuan, Minister of the Municipal Propaganda Department. The details of the meeting and the news of the memorial meetings in various districts are recorded below.

Municipal Party Headquarters

Attending Representatives: Municipal Government, Social Affairs Bureau, Garrison Headquarters, Shanghai Third Special District Transportation Workers' Union, Confucian Teaching United Association, Yutong Silk Factory Workers' Union, Pudong District Cigarette Workers' Union, Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, Municipal Public Works Bureau, Shanghai Publishing Industry Workers' Union, Shanghai Dock Workers' Union, Third District Cotton Textile Industry Workers' Union, etc., and representatives from all levels of the municipal party headquarters, totaling over seven hundred people.

Assembly Order: (1) Stand at attention, (2) Sing the Party Song, (3) Pay the highest respects to the Party flag, national flag, and the portrait of the Generalissimo, (4) The Chairman respectfully reads the Last Will and Testament, (5) Silent tribute, (6) Chairman's report, (7) Speeches, (8) Shout slogans, (9) Adjournment.

Assembly Slogans: (1) Martyr Chen's spirit will never die, (2) Continue Martyr Chen's spirit of non-compromise, (3) Commemorate Martyr Chen's steadfast belief in the Generalissimo's spirit, (4) Commemorate Martyr Chen's spirit of sacrifice for the Party, (5) Commemorate Martyr Chen's revolutionary spirit, (6) Support the Three Principles of the People, (7) Eradicate all corrupt forces, (8) Down with all imperialism, (9) Revolutionary masses unite, (10) Long live the Kuomintang of China, (11) Long live the Republic of China.

District Party Headquarters: Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the Pudong community, led by the Fifth District Party Headquarters of this city, held a memorial meeting for Mr. Chen Yingshi's martyrdom. Over sixty people attended. Chairman Zhang Zaibo gave a report, followed by speeches from representatives from all walks of life. The ceremony then concluded and adjourned. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the Jiangwan community, convened by the Seventh District Party Headquarters of this city, held a memorial meeting for Chen Yingshi's martyrdom. Dozens of people attended. Chairman Sun Letao gave a report, followed by speeches from Chen Lian'geng, Gong Minxian, Ren Huan, etc., shouting slogans and adjourning the meeting. Yesterday, under the leadership of the Ninth District Party Headquarters of this city, the Longhua community held a May 18th Memorial Meeting. Over a hundred people attended. Chairman Chen Xiaomei gave a report, followed by speeches from comrades Ru Ji, Li Mengnan, Qian Siqian, etc., before shouting slogans and adjourning the meeting. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the Meilong community, convened by the Ninth Branch of the Ninth District Party Headquarters of this city, held a memorial meeting for Mr. Chen Yingshi's martyrdom, attended by over a hundred representatives from all walks of life and local residents. Chairman Tang Shugui reported on the significance of the commemoration, followed by speeches from Wu Xiqin, etc., before shouting slogans and adjourning the meeting. Yesterday, the Two-Roads Party Headquarters held the 15th Anniversary Memorial Meeting for Mr. Chen Yingshi's martyrdom in the auditorium of the headquarters on Tiantong'an Road, attended by over a hundred representatives. Chairman Chen Chengshi reported on the circumstances of Mr. Yingshi's martyrdom, followed by speeches from comrades Chen Pin and Wei Yunlou, with very impassioned words, before shouting slogans and adjourning the meeting.

The Shanghai County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee convened the county's subordinate agencies at 9:00 AM yesterday in the auditorium to hold the 57th Generalissimo Memorial Week, followed by a memorial meeting for Mr. Chen Yingshi's martyrdom. Tang Haian Visits the Inspector-General of Customs Yesterday

Officially Sworn in One Week Later

After Liu Jiwen, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, went to Guangdong, the Ministry of Finance issued an order on the 15th, explicitly removing him from his post and simultaneously ordering Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Zhenjiang Customs, to concurrently manage the affairs of the Jianghai Customs. After receiving the order, Tang hastily took over the affairs on the morning of the 16th and separately appointed Tang Zhaoshi as secretary, Liu Fulang as head of the Tax Department, and Huang Chuwei as head of the Accounting Department. The heads of the departments under Liu's leadership rushed to hand over their responsibilities. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Tang Haian specially visited Inspector-General of Customs Frederick Maze to discuss everything. According to Tang, the handover of responsibilities by the former officials can be completed in two or three days, and he is scheduled to be officially sworn in one week later.

All Circles Support the Declaration to Abolish Unequal Treaties

Ninth District Party Headquarters: The Ninth District Party Headquarters of this city issued a declaration yesterday, stating that the National Assembly, following the Generalissimo's teachings and with a fearless spirit, resolutely and automatically announced the abolition of unequal treaties, washing away all humiliating insults, defending the survival of the Chinese nation, eliminating obstacles to global peace, and realizing the dawn of world harmony. All our compatriots, upon hearing this, were filled with joy. Recalling that since the defeat of the Sino-Japanese War, for more than eighty years, our country has been bound by unequal treaties. Our native products have been driven out by foreign goods, leading to successive bankruptcies, economic depression, and national decline to the extreme. Thinking of this, we feel extremely heartbroken. In the past, our country repeatedly proposed treaty revisions to the great powers, but those imperialists, hoping to prolong the life of unequal treaties and seeking to absorb our country's economic lifeline, evaded and delayed, and have not yet allowed it. Recently, the representatives of the National Assembly, representing the will of all the people of our country, in order to awaken the illusions of those imperialists, announced the declaration of treaty abolition to the world. All comrades in this district, as long as we have a breath left, will vow to support it to the end, regardless of any difficulties or sacrifices. We hope that all compatriots across the country will unite and support us as the government's backing. This is what we hope and pray for. We hereby declare.

Various Trade Associations: Over a hundred trade associations, including the Nanshi Native Products Industry, Floral Powder Industry, Silk and Satin Industry, Seafood and Sundries Industry, etc., yesterday issued a declaration supporting the National Assembly's declaration to abolish unequal treaties, stating: (Titles omitted) The crimes of unequal treaties not only shackle the Chinese nation but also hinder world peace. Today, the National Assembly, following the Generalissimo's teachings and based on the demands of the people, is using decisive means to automatically declare their abolition. The Chinese nation is fortunate to be rid of these shackles and is deeply gratified. Friendly countries are not lacking in people who uphold justice and righteousness, and they will also deeply sympathize with the elimination of obstacles to world peace. However, at the beginning of this abolition, if any imperialists do not reflect and realize the truth and attempt to cling to illegally seized interests, sparing no effort to obstruct and destroy, then the Chinese nation, although weak, will have the strength to deal with them fully. Merchants from all industries, who have suffered the most deeply for eighty years, are especially willing to do their utmost to vow to support the government's diplomacy as a backing, so as to thoroughly complete this task. We hereby declare, and we hope that you will understand.

Meat Merchants Throughout the City Remained Closed Yesterday

Meat Merchants in the Concession Resolved to Stop Importing Goods

The fresh meat industry in this city has been practicing slaughter cessation and business closure since the 16th due to the slaughter tax issue. Yesterday, the industry in the concession formally held a meeting and decided to act in unison from today onwards. The information obtained yesterday is recorded separately below.

Mayor's Talk: Mayor Zhang and Hu Qianxi came to Shanghai from Nanjing the day before yesterday and met with reporters who visited him to discuss the situation regarding the dispute over the collection of slaughter tax. He said, "In handling matters, I have always advocated dealing with everything in a peaceful manner and have never had any preconceptions. I have always accommodated the opinions of the public as much as possible as long as they are reasonable. According to the investigation of this slaughter tax dispute, it is not the intention of all meat merchants, but a few local ruffians and unscrupulous merchants who hope to maintain the contract donation system, using the donation money paid by the meat merchants to fill their own pockets, except for paying a small amount of donation. They know that the municipal government's recovery of self-management will greatly hinder their private interests, so they cannot help but incite and instigate disturbances. However, the citizens should understand that (1) the slaughter tax is not a new tax. This tax exists everywhere, and it has been implemented in this city for a long time. In the past, it was collected by the Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office. Recently, in order to unify the governing power, it was changed to be collected and remitted by the Shanghai Municipal Government on behalf of the office; (2) the slaughter tax rate has not increased, and the burden on meat merchants has not increased; (3) the collection procedures are striving to be simple, only providing convenience to merchants and citizens, and there is no harshness. The above are all facts, and all parties should understand them. In short, the contractor system has many drawbacks, and it is necessary to eliminate it in this era. The municipal government will never change its established principles in order to maintain the private interests of a few contractors. I hope that enlightened merchants and citizens will not be used by unscrupulous merchants, causing the disturbances to be prolonged and suffering losses themselves. I also hope that the press will uphold justice, so that the contractor system with many ills can be fundamentally eliminated."

Meat Merchants in the Concession: Over 1,100 fresh meat merchants in the public concession, such as Lu Gaojian, held a meeting yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM on Yuezhou Road. Over 200 representatives from various shops attended. First, the chairman reported on the situation of the slaughter cessation by the industry in the Chinese area due to the slaughter tax issue. Then, discussions on assistance matters began, and it was resolved to stop importing goods from today (the 19th) and prepare to close business to show assistance.

Causing Panic: Due to the slaughter cessation by the fresh meat industry for the slaughter tax issue, hotels, restaurants, meal providers, noodle shops, cake stalls, and small-scale vendors in the North and South cities and the four townships cannot buy large quantities of fresh meat in the concession due to hygiene inspection and related concerns. It is said that some fresh meat shops in the concession may also join the business closure. If this is implemented, there will be no meat to buy, so they are panicking.

Investigation of Pig Stock: After the fresh meat industry closed business, the pig industry saw a sharp decline in sales, and imported goods were less than usual. Pig merchants wired to delay the shipment to Shanghai. According to the New Voice News Agency's investigation, pig boats usually arrive in Shanghai every day, as many as 40 boats or as few as seven or eight boats. Each large boat can carry up to 200 pigs, and small boats can carry over 100 pigs. 40 pig boats arrived on the 15th, three on the 16th, and 12 on the 17th. Few arrived yesterday, and it is expected that there will be no boats arriving in Shanghai tomorrow. There are currently over 400 pigs in stock at the Xuejiabao Changyuan and other nine pig industries, and there are about 2,000 pigs on the boats in the Huangpu River from pig merchants in various places. The Longmao, Yangjing, Fuxing, Wusong, and Wanmao pig industries in Zhabei also have only over 100 pigs. The city can sell over 2,000 pigs every day, with the concession accounting for the majority.

County Slaughter Tax Replaces Recognized Merchants

County Government Proclamation Approves Wang Shoumei to Contract

The Shanghai County Government issued a proclamation yesterday, stating that the Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office instructed in order No. 392, "Regarding the county's slaughter tax, it is hereby reported that Wang Shoumei has contracted the full year tax for 4,516.66 yuan and has paid a 20% deposit. In addition to approving the merchant to contract for one year from May 1st, 20th year, to the end of April 21st year, you should immediately issue a proclamation to inform the public and order the police to provide effective assistance. This order is hereby issued, in addition to ordering the recognized merchant to comply with the order and ordering the Public Security Bureau to assist, this proclamation is hereby issued, for all slaughter industry personnel to comply with and follow. Special proclamation."

Tram Mechanics Resumed Work Yesterday

The Riri News Agency reports that the workers of the general coppersmith shop of the public concession tram company demanded the release of the arrested worker Qiao Shengfa without success, which led to a strike. The attitudes of both sides were extreme. However, after a compromise was reached the night before last, the workers secretly ordered the workers to resume work yesterday. However, due to the suddenness of the incident, some workers had not yet received the order. At 7:00 AM yesterday morning, most of the workers entered the factory, and a small number of workers did not enter the factory until after 8:00 or 9:00 AM. The damaged vehicles during the period of slowdown strike, except for a small part repaired by the factories on Hertford Road and Yangshupu, the rest were temporarily put aside. Yesterday, these vehicles were gradually sent to the general factory for repair. The work of four or five days was completed yesterday, so it was extremely busy.

Japanese Fishing Boats Cross-Border Fishing Case

Dispatching Warships to Drive Away: The Zhejiang Provincial Government received a request from the Dinghai County Magistrate, stating that recently, when local fishermen in Dinghai County were sending boats out to sea to fish, a large number of Japanese fishing boats came in groups, crossing the border and infringing, forcibly fishing within our territorial waters. In addition to ordering the Outer Sea Water Police Agency to dispatch warships to the area to protect fishermen and prevent pirates, the provincial government specially requested the Shanghai Naval Headquarters to quickly dispatch several warships to the waters of Dinghai and other places to drive away Japanese fishing boats that infringe on our maritime rights and seize our fishing industry.

Japanese Merchants Struggle: There are more than 60 Japanese fishing boats in the Yellow Sea of our country, with varying loads ranging from 40 to 100 tons. Since the National Government postponed the implementation of the ban on Japanese fishing boats entering the port, the Japanese have arbitrarily fished in the Yellow Sea, mostly in Shanghai and Qingdao. However, our country has implemented the ban on Chinese merchants selling fish on behalf of Japanese boats. Therefore, the fresh fish caught by Japanese fishing boats recently and transported to Shanghai, Qingdao, and other places for sale cannot be sold by Chinese fishermen because of the ban. On the 11th of this month, Japanese fishing boats, including the Kyoei Maru, Meiri Maru, No. 7, No. 8, Linjin Maru, and No. 1 Hoshima Maru, caught a lot of fresh fish in Wusong and Haizhou and other places, loading more than 1,000 boxes. Because they could not be sold anywhere, they had to be returned to Dalian. On the one hand, the Japanese fishing boats jointly requested the Japanese consuls in Shanghai and Qingdao to negotiate with our country to request a postponement of the ban on selling fresh fish from Japanese boats on their behalf. It is currently in progress.

Garrison Headquarters First Group Elects Group Leaders and Deputy Group Leaders

Since its establishment, the First Group of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters has been reorganized five times. Now it is time for another election, with the number of votes as the standard for election. It is reported that Zhou Baoli and Peng Chunshi received the most votes this time and were elected as the group leader and deputy group leader of this session and have been telegraphed to the special party headquarters of the Fifth Division.

Statement by Judge Gong Cheng of the French Court

At 2:30 PM yesterday afternoon, when Judge Gong Xiangsheng of the French Court was sitting in the Civil Court to hear minor civil cases, he said to the lawyers present in court, "This judge read in the newspaper today that the Lawyers Association sent a telegram to National Government Chairman Chiang, the Judicial Yuan, the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs regarding the case of recovering the Mixed Court, containing words that damage the reputation of this judge. This judge has always expressed sympathy for the recovery of this court. However, since taking office, he has handled all Chinese and foreign cases impartially, and the cases he has judged have all been handled according to law and have always been open. If you lawyers have any accusations, you must have concrete evidence and cannot speak without thinking. Regarding the issuance of arrest warrants, they have always been signed by the Chinese judge and have never been signed by the French consul alone. Today, for the sake of solemnity, in addition to making a statement first, I will also send a letter to your Lawyers Association for proper correction."
