Youth Park

Qing'e Drama Society Performs a Patriotic Heart

This is something that no one could have imagined. Beforehand, there was no sound or shadow. Suddenly, a thunderbolt from a clear sky broke through this silent Shanghai - the establishment of the Qing'e Drama Society.

Even they themselves were in a daze, and they were able to accomplish such an amazing record, which was really unexpected. Their motivation for initiating and organizing this drama society was last month - after seeing a letter from Mr. Gu Jianchen to the Shen Bao's "Art World," he said, "A Patriotic Heart" had achieved very good results in the Zhenjiang performance and was very popular among the audience. The future of Chinese new drama has released light, and the hope is very great... After they read the above facts, their competitive hearts did not allow us to hesitate any longer, and they immediately wanted to compete with the Jiangsu Provincial Educational College, which was hosted by Mr. Shigu, so they quickly gathered their comrades and immediately rehearsed "A Patriotic Heart."

As for why no one knew about it beforehand, it was because their goal was to fight and did not want to make a big fuss in advance, because past facts told us that the results were not satisfactory if we talked about it in advance, so they refused to repeat the same mistakes. Therefore, they rehearsed the drama day and night, and the people outside were sleeping in the drum, and they did not announce it to the public until the opportunity came.

This is indeed their luck and their good omen. It happened that Tongji wanted to hold a commemorative meeting on May 19 and invited them to join the performance. Of course, they would not lose this rare opportunity, so it aroused their excitement even more, and they were willing to sacrifice everything to fulfill their obligations to the drama. The results of this exercise were still able to fulfill their wishes, which gave them ten thousand times more courage.

The members of this drama society are composed of enthusiastic drama comrades from schools along the Yanjiangwan Road area. Their ambitions are great, and they are not limited to one corner. Anyone who expresses sympathy for them has the possibility of joining Qing'e.

This complicated Shanghai is enough to make us feel bored. Although there was a enthusiastic drama movement last year, and the future of the Chinese drama world seemed to have a bright future, it was not long before it disappeared and disappeared again, either because of the diversion of thought or because the organization was not sound. We are now also worried that the desert flower that has just sprouted in the desert will be blown away by a huge wind halfway through. We hope that comrades who express sympathy for the society will jointly shoulder the responsibility of nurturing.

Unimaginable

- Jianqiu

Unimaginable, because of an unimportant thing, I suddenly went to Hangzhou. The round-trip expenses did not cost me a penny. Is there such a cheap thing in the world? It really makes me feel strange.

I feel tired of the gorgeous spring. Although I have a little responsibility for the affairs, I am interested in this trip under such circumstances.

The wall clock at the station struck seven, and the locomotive's whistle wailed. Then, the wheels gradually moved, and wisps of black smoke lingered in the silent clear sky. At this time, the prosperous Shanghai gradually left me and retreated backwards.

Sitting near the car window, I closed my eyes from time to time to imagine the scenery of Hangzhou. At this time, the ancient ruins and famous scenic spots that I had long wanted to visit were spread out before me.

When the car passed Longhua, looking out from the car window, the peach blossoms of red and white intermingled on both sides of the track were swaying by the warm spring breeze, and a slight fragrance wafted towards my nostrils from time to time. Hehe, you mesmerizing peach blossoms.

"...The Wuling people have disappeared, and they are still red to people..."

The scenery changes with the distance from the city. The farther away from Shanghai, the tempting and intoxicating scenery gradually disappears before me. All that is left is the clear, leisurely, and vast suburban scenery, the vast sky, the scattered floating clouds, and the lovely green grass. When the car passed Songjiang and Jiaxing, the rapeseed flowers in the fields were densely blooming, and the bees and butterflies were recklessly trampling on the stamens. At this time, the train rushed forward rapidly, and the rumbling of the machine and the desolate long stay aroused my passionate emotions.

Corner of the Sports Field

— Ice Photography

As we neared Chang'an, the rapeseed flowers gradually thinned out. The fields on both sides had been replanted with mulberry trees. Two or three village women, bent at the waist, were cutting fresh green grass. When the train passed, they all looked up with attention. Ah, that healthy body, full muscles, and healthy eyes—this is truly the only beauty of mankind. Compared to those weak urban women who use fragrant powder to paint their faces very white in order to seduce the opposite sex, they are truly more natural and beautiful. I... ah, yes, I curse the women who use white powder to cover their original faces and seduce people, weaklings who can only consume and not produce anything.

At this time, the train was speeding forward, approaching its destination moment by moment. My heartstrings also became tense. The beautiful scenery of this ancient site and scenic spot, which I had fantasized about for so long and was finally about to realize, frequently appeared in my mind in many strange illusions.

Originally, upon arriving in Hangzhou, I would naturally have many opportunities for sightseeing. Moreover, the location where I needed to conduct business was the Kadoorie Garden by the lake, which gave me even more opportunities for sightseeing.

After a long whistle, the train arrived in Hangzhou. —Each whistle made my heartstrings tense for a moment, and this time it truly arrived. —It was already one o'clock in the afternoon. Originally, I had no luggage, so I walked leisurely out of the station empty-handed. Many rickshaw pullers came up to solicit business.

"Sir, would you like a rickshaw?"

"How much to Kadoorie Garden by West Lake?"

"Six dimes, silver coin," he stretched out a hand, gesturing the number "six" to me.

"No, four dimes, silver coin, plus fourteen copper coins. Will you go?"

"Okay, okay, I'll take you."

He respectfully lowered the rickshaw. So, I jumped in. Sitting silently in the rickshaw alone, I seemed to feel a slight loneliness. So, I asked him intentionally or unintentionally,

"Is West Lake far from here?"

"Not far," he replied breathlessly, "Not far. You'll see West Lake when we get to Qixia."

The slightly warm spring breeze brushed across my forehead, and I felt a drunken warmth in my heart. At this time, the rickshaw had arrived at Qixia, and West Lake was gradually getting closer. Ah, the dreamlike, faint green mountains embraced West Lake on three sides. The rippling lake water, half-reflected by the sunlight, reflected an even stronger light. The verdant willow branches, green and fluttering, brushed against the faces of passersby. This natural wilderness scene in spring has already given me satisfaction beyond consciousness. However, an official tour of the lake has not yet been attempted. This is the expectation of the shortest possible future.

Guidelines for Youth Garden Contributions

(1) Written works should focus on discussions of youth issues, news about domestic and foreign schools or students, essays, descriptions of school life, and personal notes. There are no restrictions on style.

(2) Illustrations should be limited to those related to youth issues.

(3) Photographs of youth life (such as sports, travel, excursions, theater, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements are all acceptable. Both individuals and groups are welcome.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) The maximum word count for each written piece is two thousand.

Book and Newspaper Reviews

Our Witness

— Zhu Jianbai

By Ms. Huiyi, published by Guanghua Bookstore

Ms. Chen Congyi, who is getting married on May 22, recently published her collection of creative works, "Our Witness." I received a complimentary copy and read it with pleasure. This collection contains five pieces of writing: 1. "Our Witness," 2. "Wutong Courtyard," 3. "Light Smoke," 4. "Eternal Regret," 5. "Doubt." Overall, the collection focuses on the sentiments of young men and women and is meticulously described in terms of technique. It is truly a work of "talent and emotion."

The most important piece of writing in the collection is, of course, her representative work, "Our Witness." This piece depicts the union of a young couple in love. From the perspective of a woman, Yun, it reflects on a current event—a pair of her friends who, united by love, separated due to misunderstandings. The man then married another woman, divorced again, and then asked the first divorced woman to take back spilled water—this really gave Yun a major stimulus. Therefore, she wanted to call off her engagement to her Ying, saying,

"Men in the world are all unreliable. His current affectionate tenderness is a hint of future trampling. Humans are selfish and self-serving, especially men. Humans are inherently weary of the old and fond of the new, especially men. Humans are originally nine-tailed foxes, cunning and deceitful. Humans are originally actors, monkeys inseparable from masks. What is liked today, who knows may be disliked tomorrow. What is disliked tomorrow, who knows may be loved the day after tomorrow..."

"Light Smoke" depicts a young girl with a heart full of helpless emotions, with a section in the middle about the interests of young girls, describing the scenery of the boudoir in a rather vivid way.

"Yifang, haven't you gotten up yet? What a lazybone!" Two people squeezed into the room. The first was the cousin Xueqin, followed by Yifen. Cousin Xueqin walked forward in three steps and wanted to drag her out, scaring her into begging,

"Give me three minutes to get out of bed."

They sat shoulder to shoulder on the sofa by the window behind the screen.

"Have you eaten breakfast?" Yifang asked while buttoning her buttons.

"I ate it early,"

"What about cousin?"

"I'm already hungry at this moment after eating it."

Xueqin always speaks so frankly, so her nickname is Miss Worry-Free.

"Miss Worry-Free, don't encounter the Worry-Free Gentleman, then it will be over," Yifang teased her like this.

"Lying in bed early in the morning, you were originally fantasizing about the Worry-Free Gentleman."

"Eternal Regret" is interspersed with the love of a loving mother and the love between the sexes. The ending, a song of eternal regret, is sincere and heartfelt, which should make all mothers in the world shed tears when they read it. Here, the author's literary foundation is fully demonstrated.

The story "Doubt" is about a student studying abroad named Yun who, because of a letter he wrote to his fiancée Ms. Li Shan in his homeland, mentioned the American woman Helena, giving Ms. Shan a major stimulus. Later, after Yun's long letter explained, the "cloud of doubt finally dissipated, welcoming Ms. Helena to China." According to my oversensitive mind, Li Shan in the article seems to be the author's pseudonym, and Yun is Ying. Whether I guessed correctly, please ask the author to tell me.

Ms. Huiyi graduated from the Faculty of Arts of Chizhi University and is currently the head of the Chinese department at Peicheng Girls' School. She has a literary talent, and her poems and lyrics are valued in the contemporary literary world. We can often read her excellent works in various newspapers and magazines. However, in the past, people admired her old literature, which reached its peak. Now, after the publication of "Our Witness," we even more praise the success of her new creations. According to the author, after "Our Witness," there will be the publication of a collection of poems titled "Green Waves," which will certainly add a large amount of vitality to the current writing world. We can only sincerely hope that "Green Waves" will be published soon, and give us a chance to read it first.
